             function setCookie(c_name, value, exdays)
             {
                 var exdate = new Date();
                 exdate.setDate(exdate.getDate() + exdays);
                 var c_value = escape(value) + ((exdays == null) ? "" : "; expires=" + exdate.toUTCString());
                 document.cookie = c_name + "=" + c_value;
             }
             function getCookie(c_name)
             {
                 var i, x, y, ARRcookies = document.cookie.split(";");
                 for (i = 0; i < ARRcookies.length; i++)
                 {
                     x = ARRcookies[i].substr(0, ARRcookies[i].indexOf("="));
                     y = ARRcookies[i].substr(ARRcookies[i].indexOf("=") + 1);
                     x = x.replace(/^\s+|\s+$/g, "");
                     if (x == c_name)
                     {
                         return unescape(y);
                     }
                 }
             }

                     positionStyle: 'fixed'

             }

   <script type="text/javascript">
    function InsertNewsLetters() {
                 var Emailid = trim(document.getElementById("varEmail").value);
                 var FristName = trim(document.getElementById("varfname").value);
                 var LastName = trim(document.getElementById("varlname").value);
                 if (Emailid == "" || FristName == "" || LastName == "") {
                     if (FristName == "") {
                         alert("Please enter first name.");
                         document.getElementById("varfname").focus();
                         return false;
                     }
                     if (LastName == "") {
                         alert("Please enter your last name.");
                         document.getElementById("varlname").focus();
                         return false;
                     }
                     if (Emailid == "" || Emailid == 'Enter Your email') {
                         alert("Please enter your email.");
                         document.getElementById("varEmail").focus();
                         return false;
                     }
                 }
                 else
                 {
                     if (validateEmail(Emailid) == false)
                     {
                         alert('Please enter valid email address.');
                         return false;
                     } else {
                         if (GetExistEmail(Emailid) == false) {
                             alert('The email address you have entered is already subscribed for our newsletter. Please enter another email address.');
                             document.getElementById("varEmail").focus();
                             document.getElementById("varEmail").value = '';
                             return false;
                         }
                         else
                         {
                             SetBackground();
                             $.ajax({
                                 type: "POST",
                                 start: SetBackground(),
                                 url: "https://www.alexandraresort.com/fronthome/sendMailtoNewsletterEmailDesktop",
                                 data: "ajax=Y&varfname=" + FristName + "&varlname=" + LastName + "&varEmail=" + Emailid + "",
                                 async: false,
                                 success: function (result)
                                 {
                                     if (result == 1)
                                     {
                                         alert("Thank You for subscribing to our Newsletter.");
                                         document.getElementById("varfname").focus();
                                         document.getElementById("varfname").value = '';
                                         document.getElementById("varlname").value = '';
                                         document.getElementById("varEmail").value = '';
                                         return false;
                                     }
                                     else
                                     {
                                         alert("Error in send mail.");
                                         document.getElementById('varEmail').reset();
                                         return false;
                                     }
                                 }
                             });
                             UnsetBackground();
                         }
                     }
                 }
                 return false;
             }
             function trim(str, chars) {
                 return ltrim(rtrim(str, chars), chars);
             }
             function ltrim(str, chars) {
                 chars = chars || "\\s";
                 return str.replace(new RegExp("^[" + chars + "]+", "g"), "");
             }
             function rtrim(str, chars) {
                 chars = chars || "\\s";
                 return str.replace(new RegExp("[" + chars + "]+$", "g"), "");
             }
             function validateEmail(email) {
                 var re = /^(([^<>()[\]\\.,;:\s@\"]+(\.[^<>()[\]\\.,;:\s@\"]+)*)|(\".+\"))@((\[[0-9]{1,3}\.[0-9]{1,3}\.[0-9]{1,3}\.[0-9]{1,3}\])|(([a-zA-Z\-0-9]+\.)+[a-zA-Z]{2,}))$/;
                 return re.test(email);
             }
             function GetExistEmail(email)
             {
                 var varEmail = email;
                 var exist;
                 $.ajax({
                     type: "POST",
                     url: "https://www.alexandraresort.com/fronthome/check_email_address",
                     data: "ajax=Y&varEmail=" + varEmail + "",
                     async: false,
                     success: function (result)
                     {
                         if (result >= 1) {
                             exist = false;
                         } else {
                             exist = true;
                         }
                     }
                 });
                 return exist;
             }
   </script>

   <script type="text/javascript">
    function SetBackground()
             {
                 $("#dvprocessing").show();
             }
             function UnSetBackGround()
             {
                 document.getElementById('dimmer').style.width = 110;
                 document.getElementById('dimmer').style.height = 0;
                 document.getElementById('dimmer').style.visibility = "";
                 document.getElementById('dvprocessing').style.display = 'none';
             }
             function getcategorydata(urldata, cid)
             {
                 var url = urldata;
                 $.ajax({
                     type: "POST",
                     url: url + "?ajax=Y&CID=" + cid,
                     async: true,
                     success: function (result)
                     {
                         var data = result.split("######");
                         document.getElementById('categorydisplay').innerHTML = data[2];
                     }
                 });
             }
   </script>

     function inquirynow_popup_check1()
     {
         $.ajax({
             type: "POST",
             url: "https://www.alexandraresort.com/fronthome/email_popup?ajax=Y",
             async: false,
             success: function (data)
             {
                 $('#popupContact').html(data)
                 disablePopup_loader();
                 initializepopupscript();
                 return false;
             }
         });
     }
     function createRequest() {
         try {
             request = new XMLHttpRequest();
         } catch (trymicrosoft) {
             try {
                 request = new ActiveXObject("Msxml2.XMLHTTP");
             } catch (othermicrosoft) {
                 try {
                     request = new ActiveXObject("Microsoft.XMLHTTP");
                 } catch (failed) {
                     request = null;
                 }
             }
         }
         if (request == null) {
             alert("Error creating request object!  Your browser does not support AJAX.  Please update it to use this site.")
         }
         ;
     }
     function checkairport(id, did)
     {
         createRequest();
         var url = "html_countries/" + id + ".html";
         if (request == null) {
             document.write("Asynchronous Request Failed");
         } else {
             request.open("GET", url, true);
             request.onreadystatechange = function () {
                 if (request.readyState == 4) {
                     document.getElementById(did).innerHTML = request.responseText;
                 }
             };
             request.send(null);
         }
     }
     function KeycheckOnlynumber(e) {
         var _dom = 0;
         _dom = document.all ? 3 : (document.getElementById ? 1 : (document.layers ? 2 : 0));
         if (document.all)
             e = window.event;
         // for IE 
         var ch = '';
         var KeyID = '';
         if (_dom == 2) {
             // for NN4
             if (e.which > 0)
                 ch = '(' + String.fromCharCode(e.which) + ')';
             KeyID = e.which;
         } else {
             if (_dom == 3) {
                 // for IE 
                 KeyID = (window.event) ? event.keyCode : e.which;
             } else {
                 // for Mozilla 
                 if (e.charCode > 0)
                     ch = '(' + String.fromCharCode(e.charCode) + ')';
                 KeyID = e.charCode;
             }
         }
         if ((KeyID >= 65 && KeyID <= 90) || (KeyID >= 97 && KeyID <= 122) || (KeyID >= 33 && KeyID <= 39) || (KeyID >= 42 && KeyID <= 42) || (KeyID == 44) || (KeyID == 43) || (KeyID == 45) || (KeyID == 40) || (KeyID == 41) || (KeyID >= 47 && KeyID <= 47) || (KeyID >= 58 && KeyID <= 64) || (KeyID >= 91 && KeyID <= 96) || (KeyID >= 123 && KeyID <= 126) || KeyID == 46) {
             return false;
         }
         return true;
     }
 
     $(document).ready(function ()
     {
         $(function () {
             $('#quick-book-date_hh').datepicker({
                 changeMonth: true,
                 changeYear: true,
                 minDate: 0,
                 dateFormat: "d-M-yy",
                 onSelect: function (date) {
                     var date2 = $('#quick-book-date_hh').datepicker('getDate');
                     date2.setDate(date2.getDate() + 7);
                     $('#quick-book-outdate_hh').datepicker('setDate', date2);
                 }
             });
             $('#quick-book-outdate_hh').datepicker({
                 changeMonth: true,
                 changeYear: true,
                 dateFormat: "d-M-yy",
                 onClose: function () {
                     var inDate = $('#quick-book-date_hh').datepicker('getDate');
                     var outDate = $('#quick-book-outdate_hh').datepicker('getDate');
                     if (outDate <= inDate) {
                         var minDate = $('#quick-book-outdate_hh').datepicker('option', 'minDate');
                         $('#quick-book-outdate_hh').datepicker('setDate', minDate);
                     }
                 }
             });
             $('#quick-book-date_hha').datepicker({
                 changeMonth: true,
                 changeYear: true,
                 minDate: 0,
                 dateFormat: "d-M-yy",
                 onSelect: function (date) {
                     var date2 = $('#quick-book-date_hha').datepicker('getDate');
                     date2.setDate(date2.getDate() + 7);
                     $('#quick-book-outdate_hha').datepicker('setDate', date2);
                 }
             });
             $('#quick-book-outdate_hha').datepicker({
                 changeMonth: true,
                 changeYear: true,
                 dateFormat: "d-M-yy",
                 onClose: function () {
                     var inDate = $('#quick-book-date_hha').datepicker('getDate');
                     var outDate = $('#quick-book-outdate_hha').datepicker('getDate');
                     if (outDate <= inDate) {
                         var minDate = $('#quick-book-outdate_hha').datepicker('option', 'minDate');
                         $('#quick-book-outdate_hha').datepicker('setDate', minDate);
                     }
                 }
             });
         });
     });
     function booking_hh() {
         var adate = $("#quick-book-date_hh").val();
         var ddate = $("#quick-book-outdate_hh").val();
         var adlt = $("#quick-book-adults_hh").val();
         var child = $("#quick-book-children_hh").val();
         var travel_agent = $("#quick-travel-agent_hh").val();
         var child_param = '';
         var promo = $("#quick-book-promo_hh").val();
         var childage_param = '';
         if (child != 0 && child > 0) {
             child_param = '&child=' + child;
             for (var jj = 1; jj <= child; jj++) {
                 var childage = '';
                 childage = $("#ChildAge_hh" + jj).val();
                 if (childage == '') {
                     alert('Please enter child ' + jj + ' age.');
                     return false;
                 } else {
                     childage_param += '&childages=' + childage;
                 }
             }
         } else {
             child_param = '';
         }
         if (promo == '') {
             var Prm = "";
         } else {
             var Prm = "&pc=" + promo;
         }
         if (travel_agent != '') {
             var IATA = "&aff=" + travel_agent;
         } else {
             var IATA = '';
         }
         var url = 'https://www.reservhotel.com/providenciales-turks-and-caicos-islands/alexandra-resort/booking-engine/ibe5.main?hotel=10474&aDate=' + adate + '&dDate=' + ddate + '&adults=' + adlt + child_param + childage_param + Prm + IATA;
         window.open(url, '_blank');
         return false;
     }
 
     function AddChild_hh(id) {
         for (var jii = 1; jii <= 5; jii++) {
             document.getElementById('divChildAge_hh' + jii).style.display = 'none';
             document.getElementById('lblChildAge_hh' + jii).style.display = 'none';
             document.getElementById('ChildAge_hh' + jii).style.display = 'none';
         }
         for (var ii = 1; ii <= id; ii++) {
             document.getElementById('divChildAge_hh' + ii).style.display = 'inline-block';
             document.getElementById('lblChildAge_hh' + ii).style.display = 'inline-block';
             document.getElementById('ChildAge_hh' + ii).style.display = 'inline-block';
         }
     }
     function booking_hha() {
         var adate = $("#quick-book-date_hha").val();
         var ddate = $("#quick-book-outdate_hha").val();
         var travel_agent = $("#quick-travel-agent_hha").val();
         var adlt = $("#quick-book-adults_hha").val();
         var child = $("#quick-book-children_hha").val();
         var child_param = '';
         var promo = $("#quick-book-promo_hha").val();
         var airport = $("#airport_hha option:selected").val();
         var fareclass = $("#fareclass_hha option:selected").val();
         var stops_check = $('#stops_hha').prop('checked');
         var show_hotels = '&showhotel=N';
         if (stops_check) {
             var stops = '&stops=0';
         } else {
             var stops = '';
         }
         var childage_param = '';
         if (child != 0 && child > 0) {
             child_param = '&child=' + child;
             for (var jj = 1; jj <= child; jj++) {
                 var childage = '';
                 childage = $("#ChildAge_hha" + jj).val();
                 if (childage == '') {
                     alert('Please enter child ' + jj + ' age.');
                     return false;
                 } else {
                     childage_param += '&childages=' + childage;
                 }
             }
         } else {
             child_param = '';
         }
         if (promo == '') {
             var Prm = "";
         } else {
             var Prm = "&pc=" + promo;
         }
         if (travel_agent != '') {
             var IATA = "&aff=" + travel_agent;
         } else {
             var IATA = '';
         }
         var url = 'https://www.reservhotel.com/providenciales-turks-and-caicos-islands/alexandra-resort/booking-engine/ibe5.main?hotel=10474&aDate=' + adate + '&dDate=' + ddate + '&adults=' + adlt + '&airport=' + airport + '&fareclass=' + fareclass + child_param + childage_param + Prm + IATA + show_hotels + stops;
         window.open(url, '_blank');
         return false;
     }
 
     function AddChild_hha(id) {
         for (var jii = 1; jii <= 5; jii++) {
             document.getElementById('divChildAge_hha' + jii).style.display = 'none';
             document.getElementById('lblChildAge_hha' + jii).style.display = 'none';
             document.getElementById('ChildAge_hha' + jii).style.display = 'none';
         }
         for (var ii = 1; ii <= id; ii++) {
             document.getElementById('divChildAge_hha' + ii).style.display = 'inline-block';
             document.getElementById('lblChildAge_hha' + ii).style.display = 'inline-block';
             document.getElementById('ChildAge_hha' + ii).style.display = 'inline-block';
         }
     }

     function inquirynow_popup_check1()
     {
         $.ajax({
             type: "POST",
             url: "https://www.alexandraresort.com/fronthome/email_popup?ajax=Y",
             async: false,
             success: function (data)
             {
                 $('#popupContact').html(data)
                 disablePopup_loader();
                 initializepopupscript();
                 return false;
             }
         });
     }

    <script type="text/javascript">
     $(document).ready(function ()
     {
 
 //        $('#quick-book-date').datepicker({
 //            minDate: 0,
 //            changeMonth: true,
 //            changeYear: true,
 //            dateFormat: "mm/dd/yy",
 //        });
 
         $(function () {
             $('#quick-book-date_h').datepicker({
                 changeMonth: true,
                 changeYear: true,
                 minDate: 0,
                 dateFormat: "d-M-yy",
                 onSelect: function (date) {
                     var date2 = $('#quick-book-date_h').datepicker('getDate');
                     date2.setDate(date2.getDate() + 7);
                     $('#quick-book-outdate_h').datepicker('setDate', date2);
                 }
             });
             $('#quick-book-outdate_h').datepicker({
                 changeMonth: true,
                 changeYear: true,
                 dateFormat: "d-M-yy",
                 onClose: function () {
                     var inDate = $('#quick-book-date_h').datepicker('getDate');
                     var outDate = $('#quick-book-outdate_h').datepicker('getDate');
                     if (outDate <= inDate) {
                         var minDate = $('#quick-book-outdate_h').datepicker('option', 'minDate');
                         $('#quick-book-outdate_h').datepicker('setDate', minDate);
                     }
                 }
             });
             $('#quick-book-date_ha').datepicker({
                 changeMonth: true,
                 changeYear: true,
                 minDate: 0,
                 dateFormat: "d-M-yy",
                 onSelect: function (date) {
                     var date2 = $('#quick-book-date_ha').datepicker('getDate');
                     date2.setDate(date2.getDate() + 7);
                     $('#quick-book-outdate_ha').datepicker('setDate', date2);
                 }
             });
             $('#quick-book-outdate_ha').datepicker({
                 changeMonth: true,
                 changeYear: true,
                 dateFormat: "d-M-yy",
                 onClose: function () {
                     var inDate = $('#quick-book-date_ha').datepicker('getDate');
                     var outDate = $('#quick-book-outdate_ha').datepicker('getDate');
                     if (outDate <= inDate) {
                         var minDate = $('#quick-book-outdate_ha').datepicker('option', 'minDate');
                         $('#quick-book-outdate_ha').datepicker('setDate', minDate);
                     }
                 }
             });
         });
     });
     function booking_h() {
         var adate = $("#quick-book-date_h").val();
         var ddate = $("#quick-book-outdate_h").val();
         var adlt = $("#quick-book-adults_h").val();
         var travel_agent = $("#quick-travel-agent_h").val();
         var child = $("#quick-book-children_h").val();
         var child_param = '';
         var promo = $("#quick-book-promo_h").val();
         var childage_param = '';
         if (child != 0 && child > 0) {
             child_param = '&child=' + child;
             for (var jj = 1; jj <= child; jj++) {
                 var childage = '';
                 childage = $("#ChildAge_h" + jj).val();
                 if (childage == '') {
                     alert('Please enter child ' + jj + ' age.');
                     return false;
                 } else {
                     childage_param += '&childages=' + childage;
                 }
             }
         } else {
             child_param = '';
         }
         if (travel_agent != '') {
             var IATA = "&aff=" + travel_agent;
         } else {
             var IATA = '';
         }
         if (promo == '') {
             var Prm = "";
         } else {
             var Prm = "&pc=" + promo;
         }
         var url = 'https://www.reservhotel.com/providenciales-turks-and-caicos-islands/alexandra-resort/booking-engine/ibe5.main?hotel=10474&aDate=' + adate + '&dDate=' + ddate + '&adults=' + adlt + child_param + childage_param + Prm + IATA;
         window.open(url, '_blank');
         return false;
     }
 
     function AddChild_h(id) {
         for (var jii = 1; jii <= 5; jii++) {
             document.getElementById('divChildAge_h' + jii).style.display = 'none';
             document.getElementById('lblChildAge_h' + jii).style.display = 'none';
             document.getElementById('ChildAge_h' + jii).style.display = 'none';
         }
         for (var ii = 1; ii <= id; ii++) {
             document.getElementById('divChildAge_h' + ii).style.display = 'inline-block';
             document.getElementById('lblChildAge_h' + ii).style.display = 'inline-block';
             document.getElementById('ChildAge_h' + ii).style.display = 'inline-block';
         }
     }
     function booking_ha() {
         var adate = $("#quick-book-date_ha").val();
         var ddate = $("#quick-book-outdate_ha").val();
         var adlt = $("#quick-book-adults_ha").val();
         var child = $("#quick-book-children_ha").val();
         var child_param = '';
         var promo = $("#quick-book-promo_ha").val();
         var travel_agent = $("#quick-travel-agent_ha").val();
         var airport = $("#airport_ha option:selected").val();
         var fareclass = $("#fareclass_ha option:selected").val();
         var stops_check = $('#stops_ha').prop('checked');
         var show_hotels = '&showhotel=N';
         if (stops_check) {
             var stops = '&stops=0';
         } else {
             var stops = '';
         }
         var childage_param = '';
         if (child != 0 && child > 0) {
             child_param = '&child=' + child;
             for (var jj = 1; jj <= child; jj++) {
                 var childage = '';
                 childage = $("#ChildAge_ha" + jj).val();
                 if (childage == '') {
                     alert('Please enter child ' + jj + ' age.');
                     return false;
                 } else {
                     childage_param += '&childages=' + childage;
                 }
             }
         } else {
             child_param = '';
         }
         if (promo == '') {
             var Prm = "";
         } else {
             var Prm = "&pc=" + promo;
         }
         if (travel_agent != '') {
             var IATA = "&aff=" + travel_agent;
         } else {
             var IATA = '';
         }
         var url = 'https://www.reservhotel.com/providenciales-turks-and-caicos-islands/alexandra-resort/booking-engine/ibe5.main?hotel=10474&aDate=' + adate + '&dDate=' + ddate + '&adults=' + adlt + '&airport=' + airport + '&fareclass=' + fareclass + child_param + childage_param + Prm + IATA + show_hotels + stops;
         window.open(url, '_blank');
         return false;
     }
 
     function AddChild_ha(id) {
         for (var jii = 1; jii <= 5; jii++) {
             document.getElementById('divChildAge_ha' + jii).style.display = 'none';
             document.getElementById('lblChildAge_ha' + jii).style.display = 'none';
             document.getElementById('ChildAge_ha' + jii).style.display = 'none';
         }
         for (var ii = 1; ii <= id; ii++) {
             document.getElementById('divChildAge_ha' + ii).style.display = 'inline-block';
             document.getElementById('lblChildAge_ha' + ii).style.display = 'inline-block';
             document.getElementById('ChildAge_ha' + ii).style.display = 'inline-block';
         }
     }
    </script>

         $('#scrollTop').click(function (e) {
             e.preventDefault();
             var target = this.hash;
             $target = $(target);
             setTimeout(function () {
                 $('html, body').stop().animate({
                     'scrollTop': ($target.offset().top - 106)
                 }, 2000, 'swing');
             }, 1);
         });
